        script.setAttribute("async", "async");
        script.src = ('https:' == document.location.protocol ? 'https:' : 'http:') + '//vw-sync2ad-delivery.s3.amazonaws.com/SDK-JS/1.0/release/1.0.3/sync2ad.js';
        script.onreadystatechange = script.onload = function () {
            if (!s2ad_loaded && (!script.readyState || /loaded|complete/.test(script.readyState))) {
                s2ad_loaded = true;
                Sync2Ad.start({
                    endpoint: 'https://vw-sync2ad-prod.s3.amazonaws.com',                   //v.Mobile 
                    //endpoint: 'https://vw-sync2ad-preprod-client.s3.amazonaws.com',       //v.Desktop
                    siteId: 'larous'
                });
            }
        };
        document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(script);
